Came here on a last minute adventure. First off our waitress Tammy was incredible. We were seated outside on their beautiful brick patio and she was the only one serving 7 full tables. <Rating>4<//Rating><review>My usual nail salon is closed on Mondays and I needed a manicure for an event the next day, so I ended up at Polka Dot Nails after seeing a ton of great reviews online.
Service was friendly. The inside didn't have music blaring like some places and it was calming & quiet even though it was packed. The massage chair worked well and everything seemed clean and the color selection was good. I got a regular spa pedicure and a gel polish manicure.
The pedicure was good, no complaints. Basic and everything a spa pedicure usually entails.
The manicure cost less than my normal place that Only does gel which was fine, but now I know why- One of my nails (so, with GEL polish) Chipped after 2 days. (Gel polish is designed to Not do that.)
So, that's a bit frustrating. Plus, the UV gel dryers- both if then were having issues that day and I wonder if the polish didn't get to set correctly/thoroughly (?) there has to be a reason for the polish chipping because it's definitely not due to extensive wear & tear on my part. So that's my only real "complaint" - which is more so just a minor annoyance not a complaint. The experience as a whole and regarding the actual salon was not "bad" at all.
Cons: The parking lot is really tiny, and they ONLY take cash tips so I had to go across the street to find an ATM so I could tip. Granted, they took me as a walk -in and I didn't have to wait even though they were quite busy.
Pros: It's a good nail salon and I would go there again if the need arose, friendly & thorough service (no rushing to get me in & out or not doing a good job due to rushing)
...but even as I type this I'm looking at my chipped nail and feeling a little bit salty about it. I didn't spend $30 on a manicure to have it last 48 hours....</review>< Pics>
